# Daily Briefings — Analysis Summaries

Trading analysis and recommendations based on each day's scan data.

---

## Update Protocol

**Trigger:** After updating `metrics-logs.md` with the day's raw data.

**Steps:**
1. Analyse the metrics — compare against previous day(s) for trends
2. Present analysis and trade recommendations to the user in chat
3. After user discussion, write the briefing entry here
4. Insert new entry **at the top** of the log (immediately below the `---` after this protocol section)

**Entry format:**
```
## YYYY-MM-DD (Day of week)

**Regime:** [NBA regime] ([phase/qualifier]) | **Tradeable:** [X]S / [Y]C | **Avg VRP:** [value]

[1-2 paragraph narrative analysis covering: regime shifts, top signals, key movements from
previous day, earnings impacts, sector themes, data quality notes if any]

**Position: [specific recommendations with RV Accel Status / environment cleanliness; contract count is the trader's call, recorded in the trade journal]**
```

**Analysis should cover:**
- Regime status and any shifts from previous day
- Top SELL and CONDITIONAL signals with scores
- Day-over-day changes for key tickers (score, VRP, slope, regime changes)
- Earnings gate impacts (newly gated/ungated tickers)
- Aggregate stats (avg VRP, % negative VRP, RV accel trends)
- Any data quality issues observed
- Actionable position recommendations referencing **RV Accel Status** (Excellent / Good / Acceptable / Caution / Avoid · Wait). Position size is a trader-controlled decision recorded in the trade journal — not prescribed by the dashboard or this briefing.

**Tone:** Concise, data-driven, opinionated. Reference specific numbers. Flag uncertainty.

---

> **IMPORTANT:** Entries are in **descending order** (newest first). New entries go immediately below this line.

---

Today, the Locked VRP Re-Fattening 13.4 → 15.1 the WIDEST Tradeable Fuel on the Board — but the Accel Comes Back WARM at 1.07, One Tick From the 1.10 Hard Exit, Hotter Than at Any Point of Its First **The wall ran backward — for the first time in the record, the calendar gave one back: SBUX resurrected 0 → 69, TOP SELL again, the print that stood 13d away yesterday standing 18d today, the locked VRP re-fattening 13.4 → 15.1, the widest tradeable fuel on the board — the cycle's defining trade handed back two sessions after the wall took it.** But it came back changed: the slope is clean again at 0.90 (the 1.19 pre-print pop leaving with the date), while the accel returned at 1.07 — one tick from the 1.10 hard exit, hotter than at any point of a first life it spent at 0.93–0.96. And the calendar axis itself wobbled twice in one session: XOM — scheduled to zero TODAY at 15d — printed 21d instead, and CAT, HD, and MCD all flipped to TBD; the wall has called every exit one-for-one since 7/15, but the dates underneath it just proved movable, and that cuts both ways. **The louder return is NFLX: 0 → 68 off Thursday's print carrying a 26.1 VRP — the widest the record has EVER produced, nearly double SBUX's cycle peak — on a sub-1.0 accel (0.89) and a 95d runway: the exact letter of the refill trigger this book has waited on since the wall started taking names, and it's UNTOUCHABLE — the lone DANGER, its slope coming through the event LOUDER than it went in (2.05 → 2.12), skew −30.0 an outlier without precedent, IV parked at the 99th percentile AFTER earnings.** That's the anti-crush — the first post-print name to come back richer than it went in, the market refusing to release whatever the print didn't resolve. **The sixth cross printed the strongest fuel of the entire record — −0.9 → +1.1, a 2.0-point swing past 7/14's +1.0 high — and it is two names deep: breadth healed only 61% → 58% negative, still a majority, and the decomposition is brutal — strip NFLX and the average goes flat, strip SBUX with it and the universe is −0.7.** Background by the five-failure rule, and the rule never had a better exhibit. **The structure handed the trophy back on **Position:** Two called shots landed and one axis broke, and the ledger opens with all three: the second PLAYOFFS died in exactly one session as priced, UBER's Day-2 gate resolved pass exactly as scripted — and the calendar, the one axis that had called every exit to the day, moved twice in a single session, so runways are now estimates to verify, not clocks to trust. The discipline at the top is unchanged and freshly armored: you do not sell this universe at +1.1 when the print is two names deep on 58% breadth — the sixth cross is background by the five-failure rule, and today's decomposition (flat ex-NFLX, −0.7 ex-both) is the best argument the rule has ever had; it earns attention only on a multi-session hold with breadth THROUGH 50%, and 58% isn't it. The edge that pays remains name-specific width behind clean structure, and for the first time since 7/14 there are four names carrying it. **PLTR** — the lead, and no longer the whole book: the Day-3 pass came with every axis improving, the 8.7 → 11.7 re-widening reversing the exact fade-shaped warning set as the exit, the 0.59 accel the coolest on the tradeable tier; carry it as the anchor (weight is your call — the framework says it has re-earned everything asked of it three sessions running), harvest-fast frame unchanged, roughly three sessions to a wall whose dates just proved movable in both directions — verify the 17d rather than trusting it; θ/V warming 1.13 → 1.23 is the standing hot caveat. **SBUX** — re-entry is a decision, not an inheritance: the framework says TOP SELL and the edge genuinely came back (15.1, essentially the 15.4 it locked at), the slope clean at 0.90 — but the accel returned at 1.07, one tick under the hard exit, and the guidance is probe-sized re-entry rather than former full weight, with three tripwires: through 1.10 exits before the position is warm, a cool back under ~1.0 re-earns the old size, and any calendar re-revision back inside 14d is an immediate scratch — the axis that gave it back can take it back. **UBER** — the pass earns exactly what yesterday's script offered: second probe behind PLTR, probe-sized, on 6.5 / 0.77 / 0.90 / 19d; the +5.2 / −0.4 / +5.9 / +6.5 history keeps the leash short — a fade toward flat or an accel through 1.0 un-earns it same-day. **WMT** — the different-shaped third: thinnest fuel (+3.5) behind the cleanest twin axes of the book (0.84 / 0.84) and the longest runway anywhere (34d) — the only campaign candidate on a board of sprints; smallest probe or watch-for-width, and the 0.5 → 3.5 fattening continuing is what upgrades it — it's also the one name where the wall isn't the clock. **NFLX** — the trap of the cycle, named as such: 26.1 on a sub-1.0 accel and 95d is the letter of the refill trigger and the spirit of nothing — the curve came through the event louder, the −30 skew is pricing something the print didn't resolve, and post-earnings IV at the 99th percentile is the anti-crush. AVOID, absolute. But make it the premier watch of the cycle: if that slope normalizes under 1.0 with even half the 26.1 intact, it's the biggest trade the record has ever offered — and the refill trigger formally gains its missing clause today: positive VRP under a sub-1.0 accel on a long runway AND a clean curve. **QQQ / SPY** — score-watches, no positions: −4.5 narrowing and −0.7 dead flat on the deepest contango anywhere; they arm on a cross to positive, and SPY is closer than it's ever been while still having nothing to sell. **EEM / XLE / XOM** — the trio resolves into one answer: EEM re-inverted exactly as degree-not-kind warned, off the watch; XLE is the lone genuine heal (0.92, deepening) but +1.3 is thin — bench it in the probe queue behind WMT; XOM was handed six extra days and did nothing with them (+0.7, accel 1.13) — pass, the month-old whipsaw now has more runway to keep not resolving. **JNJ / GS / JPM / XLF** — the refill ledger holds the trigger's pieces in different hands: JNJ the curve (0.94, first of the cohort) without the accel or the fuel (1.14, −5.8); GS neither — the record's deepest crush still crushing on the board's hottest accel, do not catch it; JPM the structure without the fuel (0.96, −0.9); XLF quietly closest to whole (0.98, +1.1, slope 0.73). Nobody assembles it yet, and the wall cohort re-supplies the bin from 5d out — GOOG and TSLA print within the week wearing building inversions. **CPS** — 1 back at construction, 0 actionable, still the last thing to re-arm; and the overlay is the session's real message: VVIX through 100 at a second straight record, VIX up 3.1 in two sessions, the contango spread nearly halved — printing INTO the record fuel read. When the vol-of-vol record and the fuel record disagree, believe the one that isn't propped by two tickers. Forward watchpoints: (1) SBUX's accel at 1.07 — the entire re-entry is this one number; under 1.0 re-earns full weight, through 1.10 ends it. (2) PLTR into the wall in ~3 sessions — the exit warning reset today; the sequence to respect is a fresh narrowing plus a warming accel, and hard-check the 17d date. (3) Calendar integrity — two revisions and three TBDs in one session; verify every runway before leaning on it, and treat a SBUX re-revision as a position event, not a data note. (4) NFLX's slope — 2.12 → sub-1.0 with the VRP holding is the next defining trade. (5) The sixth cross — multi-session hold with breadth through 50% or it's noise; 58% and two names deep says noise. (6) Stress 33.3% — the doubling that survives the NFLX strip lives in the refill cohort's accels; if that heat migrates back into the tradeable tier, the 7/6 shape is reloading, and slope 0.955 drifting at the 1.0 line is where it shows first. Honest framing: yesterday closed by saying the next real book comes from the post-print names, and the first positive VRP under a clean accel over there is the trade — today the tape delivered that exact trigger and attached the loudest structural veto of the record to it, then handed back the trade the wall had already taken, while the regime returned its trophy in one session, again. The book is the deepest of the cycle — one resurrected SELL wearing a nearly-fired exit, three conditionals that each passed a gate the graveyard says most names fail, two watches with no fuel — sitting under a record fuel print that is two names of illusion and a vol-of-vol gauge making records the other way. Trust the gates, not the gauge: the gates built this book, and the gauge is now oh-for-six.
